<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Strong Overall SSRS Performance and Growing Operating Profit Despite Mix Shift to Cloud Subscription:</B> Non-IFRS Software and Software-Related

<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Full Year Outlook Reflecting Accelerated Shift to the Cloud:</B> Raising Non-IFRS Cloud Subscriptions and Support Revenue Outlook to &#128;1,040
&#150; &#128;1,070 Million and Now Expecting Non-IFRS Operating Profit Outlook in a Range of &#128;5.6&nbsp;- &#128;5.8 Billion at Constant Currencies </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><I>WALLDORF, Germany &#150; October&nbsp;20, 2014 &#150;</I></B> <U>SAP SE</U> (NYSE: SAP) today announced its financial results for the third quarter and nine months ended September&nbsp;30, 2014.
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>BUSINESS HIGHLIGHTS IN THE THIRD QUARTER 2014 </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">SAP again delivered strong growth in the cloud and a solid overall revenue performance. With non-IFRS cloud subscriptions and support revenue increasing 41% (42% at constant currencies) SAP is the fastest
growing enterprise cloud company at scale</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1"><SUP STYLE="vertical-align:baseline; position:relative; bottom:.8ex">1</SUP></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">. <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-IFRS</FONT> software and software-related service revenue grew 7% (7% at constant currencies). The negative effects from currency translation SAP experienced year-to-date dissipated in the third quarter and are
expected to reverse in the fourth quarter 2014. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="line-height:8px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:2px;border-bottom:0.5pt solid #000000;width:10%">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1"><SUP STYLE="vertical-align:baseline; position:relative; bottom:.8ex">1</SUP>&nbsp;</FONT><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Compared to SAP&#146;s peer group companies with an enterprise software annual cloud revenue run rate above &#128;1 billion. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TR>
<TD VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><I>SAP Reports Third Quarter and Nine Months 2014 Results</I></B></FONT></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD VALIGN="top" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><I> Page
 2
</I></FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <p STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P>
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#147;We are accelerating our shift to the cloud with more than 40% revenue growth in the cloud. SAP is
THE cloud company powered by SAP HANA helping customers run simple with over 44&nbsp;million cloud users and the world&#146;s largest business network. We are leading the next generation customer engagement with the triple digit growth of our
omni-channel e-commerce platform,&#148; said Bill McDermott of SAP. &#147;Our portfolio depth in the cloud, global scale and industry domain expertise are the bedrocks that separate us in the marketplace. With SAP HANA and the Business Network, SAP
will continue to shape the future of the enterprise software industry.&#148; </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#147;We achieved a solid overall topline performance in the
quarter with 7% growth in non-IFRS software and software-related service revenue. Year-to-date non-IFRS software and software-related service revenue is up 8% at constant currencies &#150; at the high end of our full-year outlook range. Non-IFRS
earnings per share increased 8% in the quarter,&#148; said Luka Mucic, CFO of SAP. &#147;Our order entry for new business in the cloud was more than one third of the software license revenue in the third quarter, up significantly from a year ago.
With this powerful shift we are raising the cloud outlook again while adjusting the operating income range to reflect less upfront and more ratable revenue.&#148; </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">SAP&#146;s annual cloud revenue run rate now exceeds &#128;1.3
billion</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1"><SUP STYLE="vertical-align:baseline; position:relative; bottom:.8ex">2</SUP></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"> or $1.7 billion</FONT><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1"><SUP STYLE="vertical-align:baseline; position:relative; bottom:.8ex">3</SUP></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">. Non-IFRS calculated cloud billings</FONT><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1"><SUP STYLE="vertical-align:baseline; position:relative; bottom:.8ex">4</SUP></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"> increased 51% (27% at constant currencies). Non-IFRS deferred cloud
subscriptions and support revenue was &#128;498&nbsp;million as of September&nbsp;30, 2014, a year-over-year increase of 30% (22% at constant currencies). SAP&#146;s cloud applications total subscribers now exceed 44 million. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">SAP is driving next generation customer engagement. Its hybris omni-channel e-commerce platform in combination with Cloud for Sales had another quarter
of triple-digit growth in software revenue and cloud subscriptions and support revenue. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">SAP is in the lead in the transformation to the
global &#147;Network Economy&#148; with over 1.6&nbsp;million connected companies on the world&#146;s largest cloud-based business trading community. Trailing twelve month network spend
volume</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1"><SUP STYLE="vertical-align:baseline; position:relative; bottom:.8ex">5</SUP></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"> was close to $600 billion &#150; more than Amazon,
eBay and Alibaba all combined. The planned addition of Concur would amplify the &#147;network effect&#148; and ecosystem with broad reach into the US$1.2 trillion corporate travel market. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">SAP saw continued broad market adoption of SAP HANA, the Real-Time Business Platform, across all industries and regions as customers realize the compelling business benefits of SAP HANA. SAP HANA is at
the core of the Company&#146;s &#147;Run Simple&#148; strategy: integrating all SAP solutions on ONE business platform in the Cloud. SAP now has more than 4,100 SAP HANA customers and more than 1,450 customers for SAP Business Suite on HANA. SAP
HANA is also evolving into the leading development platform with more than 1,600 startup companies building applications on SAP HANA. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="line-height:8px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:2px;border-bottom:0.5pt solid #000000;width:10%">&nbsp;</P>

<TD VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><I>SAP Reports Third Quarter and Nine Months 2014 Results</I></B></FONT></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD VALIGN="top" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><I> Page
 3
</I></FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <p STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P>
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Third Quarter 2014 Regional Revenue </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">SAP had a solid performance in EMEA, despite uncertainties in the Ukraine and the Middle East. Non-IFRS software and software-related service revenue increased 8% (8% at constant currencies) with a strong
performance in Germany in both software and cloud subscriptions and support revenue. Non-IFRS cloud subscriptions and support revenue in EMEA was a particular highlight, growing 59% (59% at constant currencies), showing exceptional cloud traction in
Europe. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Americas region saw a mixed performance in Latin America. Similar to other companies in the industry SAP is seeing a more
difficult macro and political environment in Latin America, in particular in Brazil and Argentina, combined with execution issues. Non-IFRS software and software-related service revenue in the Americas increased 5% (5% at constant currencies).
Non-IFRS cloud subscriptions and support revenue grew by 34% (34% at constant currencies). </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Asia Pacific Japan (APJ) region had a strong
performance with 10% growth in non-IFRS software and software-related service revenue (10% at constant currencies). Non-IFRS cloud subscriptions and support revenue grew by 57% (56% at constant currencies). SAP achieved a turnaround in its business
in Japan with solid double-digit growth. </FONT></P>

million), an increase of 45%. Non-IFRS cloud subscriptions and support revenue was &#128;278&nbsp;million (2013: &#128;197 million), an increase of 41% (42% at constant currencies). IFRS software and support revenue was &#128;3.32 billion (2013:
&#128;3.16 billion), an increase of 5%. Non-IFRS software and support revenue was &#128;3.32 billion (2013: &#128;3.17 billion), an increase of 5% (5% at constant currencies). IFRS software and software-related service revenue was &#128;3.60 billion
(2013: &#128;3.35 billion), an increase of 7%. Non-IFRS software and software-related service revenue was &#128;3.60 billion (2013: &#128;3.36 billion), an increase of 7% (7% at constant currencies). IFRS total revenue was &#128;4.25 billion (2013:
&#128;4.05 billion), an increase of 5%. Non-IFRS total revenue was &#128;4.26 billion (2013: &#128;4.06 billion), an increase of 5% (5% at constant currencies). </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">IFRS operating profit was &#128;1.16 billion (2013: &#128;1.04 billion), an increase of 11%. Non-IFRS operating profit was &#128;1.36 billion (2013: &#128;1.30 billion), an increase of 5% (3% at constant
currencies). IFRS operating margin was 27.2% (2013: 25.8%), an increase of 1.4 percentage points. Non-IFRS operating margin was 31.8% (2013: 32.0%), a decrease of 0.1 percentage points (0.5 percentage points at constant currencies). </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">IFRS profit after tax was &#128;881&nbsp;million (2013: &#128;762 million), an increase of 16%. Non-IFRS profit after tax was &#128;1.01 billion (2013:
&#128;933 million), an increase of 8%. IFRS basic earnings per share was &#128;0.74 (2013: &#128;0.64), an increase of 15%. Non-IFRS basic earnings per share was &#128;0.84 (2013: &#128;0.78), an increase of 8%. The IFRS and non-IFRS effective tax
rates in the third quarter of 2014 were 26.5% (2013: 26.4%) and 27.7% (2013: 27.6%), respectively. </FONT></P>

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">1)</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">All figures are unaudited. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">2)</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">For a detailed description of SAP&#146;s non-IFRS measures see <U>Explanation of Non-IFRS Measures</U> online. For a breakdown of the individual adjustments see page F8
in the appendix to this press release. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">IFRS cloud subscriptions and support revenue was &#128;738&nbsp;million (2013: &#128;488
million), an increase of 51%. Non-IFRS cloud subscriptions and support revenue was &#128;741&nbsp;million (2013: &#128;547 million), an increase of 35% (40% at constant currencies). IFRS software and support revenue was &#128;9.39 billion (2013:
&#128;9.08 billion), an increase of 3%. Non-IFRS software and support revenue was &#128;9.40 billion (2013: &#128;9.10 billion), an increase of 3% (6% at constant currencies). IFRS software and software-related service revenue was &#128;10.13
billion (2013: &#128;9.57 billion), an increase of 6%. Non-IFRS software and software-related service revenue was &#128;10.14 billion (2013: &#128;9.65 billion), an increase of 5% (8% at constant currencies). IFRS total revenue was &#128;12.10
billion (2013: &#128;11.71 billion), an increase of 3%. Non-IFRS total revenue was &#128;12.11 billion (2013: &#128;11.78 billion), an increase of 3% (5% at constant currencies). </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">IFRS operating profit was &#128;2.58 billion (2013: &#128;2.68 billion), a decrease of 4%. Non-IFRS operating profit was &#128;3.51 billion (2013: &#128;3.39 billion), an increase of 4% (6% at constant
currencies). IFRS operating margin was 21.3% (2013: 22.9%), a decrease of 1.6 percentage points. Non-IFRS operating margin was 29.0% (2013: 28.7%), an increase of 0.3 percentage points (0.1 percentage points at constant currencies). </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">IFRS profit after tax was &#128;1.97 billion (2013: &#128;2.01 billion), a decrease of 2%. Non-IFRS profit after tax was &#128;2.62 billion (2013:
&#128;2.47 billion), an increase of 6%. IFRS basic earnings per share was &#128;1.65 (2013: &#128;1.68), a decrease of 2%. Non-IFRS basic earnings per share was &#128;2.19 (2013: &#128;2.08), an increase of 6%. The IFRS and non-IFRS effective tax
rates in the nine months of 2014 were 24.8% (2013: 23.4%) and 26.4% (2013: 25.6%), respectively. </FONT></P>

<p Style='page-break-before:always'>

<TABLE CELLSPACING="0" CELLPADDING="0" WIDTH="100%" BORDER="0" STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" ALIGN="center">

<TD VALIGN="bottom" WIDTH="3%"></TD>
<TD WIDTH="34%"></TD></TR>
<TR>
<TD VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><I>SAP Reports Third Quarter and Nine Months 2014 Results</I></B></FONT></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD VALIGN="top" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><I> Page
 6
</I></FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <p STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P>
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Cash Flow &#150; Nine Months 2014 </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Operating cash flow was &#128;3.08 billion (2013: &#128;3.04 billion), an increase of 1% year-over-year. Free cash flow was &#128;2.61 billion (2013: &#128;2.64 billion), a decrease of 1% year-over-year.
Free cash flow was 22% of total revenue (2013: 23%). At September&nbsp;30, 2014, SAP had a total group liquidity of &#128;3.40 billion (December 31, 2013: &#128;2.84 billion), which includes cash and cash equivalents and short term investments. Net
liquidity at September&nbsp;30, 2014 was -&#128;1.01 billion compared to -&#128;1.47 billion at December&nbsp;31, 2013. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>BUSINESS OUTLOOK
2014 </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Company updated its outlook for the full year 2014. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Based on the strong momentum in SAP&#146;s cloud business, the Company is raising its cloud outlook again and now expects full year 2014 non-IFRS cloud subscriptions and support revenue to be in a range
of &#128;1,040 &#150; &#128;1,070&nbsp;million (previously &#128;1,000 &#150; &#128;1,050 million) at constant currencies (2013: &#128;757 million). The upper end of this range represents a growth rate of 41%. The Company continues to expect full
year 2014 non-IFRS software and software-related service revenue to increase by 6% &#150; 8% at constant currencies (2013: &#128;14.03 billion). </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">With the customer-driven mix shift from upfront to cloud subscription revenue the Company now expects full-year 2014 non-IFRS operating profit to be in a range of &#128;5.6 billion &#150; &#128;5.8
billion (previously &#128;5.8 &#150; &#128;6.0 billion) at constant currencies (2013: &#128;5.48 billion). </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">SAP anticipates the fast-growing
cloud business along with growth in support revenue will drive a higher proportion of more predictable revenue in the future. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The 2014
business outlook does not include any contributions from the planned addition of Concur Technologies, Inc. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">While the Company&#146;s full-year
2014 business outlook is at constant currency, actual currency reported figures are expected to continue to be impacted by currency exchange rate fluctuations. If exchange rates remain at the September 2014 level for the rest of the year, the
Company expects non-IFRS software and software-related service revenue and non-IFRS operating profit growth rates at actual currency to experience a positive currency impact of approximately 3 percentage points and 3 percentage points respectively
for the fourth quarter of 2014 and a negative currency effect of approximately 1 percentage points and neutral impact respectively for the full year 2014. </FONT></P>

<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1">*</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1">Adjustments in the revenue line items are for support revenue, cloud subscriptions and support revenue, and other similarly recurring revenues that entities acquired by
SAP would have recognized had they remained stand-alone entities but that SAP is not permitted to recognize as revenue under IFRS as a result of business combination accounting rules. Adjustments in the operating expense line items are for
acquisition-related charges, share-based payment expenses, restructuring expenses, as well as the TomorrowNow and Versata litigation expenses. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1">**</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1">Constant currency revenue and operating income figures are calculated by translating revenue and operating income of the current period using the average exchange rates
from the previous year&#146;s respective period instead of the current period. Constant currency period-over-period changes are calculated by comparing the current year&#146;s non-IFRS constant currency numbers with the non-IFRS number of the
previous year&#146;s respective period. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">For a more detailed description of these adjustments and their limitations as well as
our constant currency figures, see our Web site www.sap.com/corporate-en/investors/newsandreports/reporting-framework.epx under &#147;Non-IFRS Measures and Estimates&#148;. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Due to rounding, numbers may not add up precisely. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>EXPLANATION OF NON-IFRS ADJUSTMENTS

<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1">*</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1">Adjustments in the revenue and deferred revenue line items are for cloud subscriptions and support revenue, and other similarly recurring revenues that entities
acquired by SAP would have recognized had they remained stand-alone entities but that SAP is not permitted to recognize as revenue under IFRS as a result of business combination accounting rules. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1">**</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1">Constant currency revenue figures are calculated by translating revenue of the current period using the average exchange rates from the previous year&#146;s respective
period instead of the current period. Constant currency deferred revenue balances are calculated by translating the current period&#146;s opening and closing deferred revenue balances as well as the comparative period&#146;s closing deferred revenue
balance using the opening exchange rates of the comparative period. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">For a more detailed description of these adjustments and
their limitations as well as our constant currency figures, see our Web site www.sap.com/corporate-en/investors/newsandreports/reporting-framework.epx under &#147;Non-IFRS Measures and Estimates&#148;. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Due to rounding, numbers may not add up precisely. </FONT></P>

<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">*</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Adjustments in the revenue line items are for support revenue, cloud subscriptions and support revenue, and other similarly recurring revenues that entities acquired by
SAP would have recognized had they remained stand-alone entities but that SAP is not permitted to recognize as revenue under IFRS as a result of business combination accounting rules. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">**</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Constant currency revenue figures are calculated by translating revenue of the current period using the average exchange rates from the previous year&#146;s respective
period instead of the current period. Constant currency period-over-period changes are calculated by comparing the current year&#146;s non-IFRS constant currency numbers with the non-IFRS number of the previous year&#146;s respective period.
</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">For a more detailed description of these adjustments and their limitations as well as our constant currency figures, see our
Web site www.sap.com/corporate-en/investors/newsandreports/reporting-framework.epx under &#147;Non-IFRS Measures and Estimates&#148;. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Due to
rounding, numbers may not add up precisely. </FONT></P>
